    SELECT DISTINCT [a].[INVMLO_Id], [b].[INVMSI_Id], [a].[INVMLO_LocationRoomName], [a].[INVMLO_LocationRemarks], [a].[INVMLO_InchargeName], [a].[HRME_Id], LTRIM(RTRIM((CASE

        WHEN [c].[HRME_EmployeeFirstName] IS NULL OR ([c].[HRME_EmployeeFirstName] = N'')
        THEN N'' ELSE N' ' + [c].[HRME_EmployeeFirstName]
    END + CASE
        WHEN ([c].[HRME_EmployeeMiddleName] IS NULL OR ([c].[HRME_EmployeeMiddleName] = N'')) OR ([c].[HRME_EmployeeMiddleName] = N'0')
        THEN N'' ELSE N' ' + [c].[HRME_EmployeeMiddleName]
    END) + CASE
        WHEN ([c].[HRME_EmployeeLastName] IS NULL OR ([c].[HRME_EmployeeLastName] = N'')) OR ([c].[HRME_EmployeeLastName] = N'0')
        THEN N'' ELSE N' ' + [c].[HRME_EmployeeLastName]
    END)) AS [employeename]
    FROM [INV].[INV_Master_Location] AS [a]
    CROSS JOIN [INV].[INV_Master_Site] AS [b]
    CROSS JOIN [HR_Master_Employee] AS [c]
    WHERE (((([a].[INVMSI_Id] = [b].[INVMSI_Id]) AND ([a].[HRME_Id] = [c].[HRME_Id])) AND ([a].[MI_Id] = [b].[MI_Id])) AND ([a].[MI_Id] = @__data_MI_Id_0)) AND ([a].[INVMLO_Id] = @__data_INVMLO_Id_1)
